    SPICEKernels.SPICEKernels — Module

    Download any and all Generic Kernels provided by NASA JPL!

    Warning

    This package is not affiliated with or endorsed by NASA, JPL, or any other organization! This is an independently written package by an astrodynamics hobbyist.

    SPICEKernels.DSK — Type
    struct DSK <: SPICEKernels.DigitalShapeKernel

    A digital shape kernel.

    source
    SPICEKernels.DigitalShapeKernel — Type
    abstract type DigitalShapeKernel <: SPICEKernels.SPICEKernel

    A supertype representing Digital Shape Kernels (DSK).

    source
    SPICEKernels.EphemerisKernel — Type
    abstract type EphemerisKernel <: SPICEKernels.SPICEKernel

    A supertype representing Spacecraft and Planet Kernels, also known as ephemeris kernels (SPK).

    source

    SPICEKernels.PCK — Type
    struct PCK <: SPICEKernels.PlanetaryConstantsKernel

    A planetary constants kernel.

    source
    SPICEKernels.PlanetaryConstantsKernel — Type
    abstract type PlanetaryConstantsKernel <: SPICEKernels.SPICEKernel

    A supertype representing Planetary Constants Kernels (PCK).

    source
    SPICEKernels.SPICEKernel — Type
    abstract type SPICEKernel

    A supertype for all SPICE Kernels! To satisfy the SPICEKernel interface, your new type must implement each of the methods below.

    • SPICEKernels.type(kernel)::AbstractString
    • SPICEKernels.path(kernel)::AbstractString
    source
    SPICEKernels.SPK — Type
    struct SPK <: SPICEKernels.EphemerisKernel

    A planetary & spacecraft ephemeris kernel.

    source
    SPICEKernels.fetchkernel — Method
    fetchkernel(kernel; directory, ignorecache)

    Given the ephemeris file name, download the file to the SPICEKernels.jl scratch space, and return a path to the file location. If a full URL or path is provided, that path will be used. Otherwise, the kernel is assumed to be a SPICE Generic Kernel.

    Extended Help

    If ignorecache is is enabled, the ephemeris file will be re-downloaded even if it exists already in the SPICEKernels.jl scratch space. If directory is set to something other than the SPICEKernels.SPICE_KERNEL_DIR variable, the file is downloaded to the provided directory instead of the SPICEKernels.jl scratch space.

    source
    SPICEKernels.kernel — Method
    kernel(path)

    Construct a SPICEKernel instance, with the type informed by the provided file's extension.

    source
    SPICEKernels.path — Function

    Return the path to the kernel. This can be a URL!

    source
    SPICEKernels.type — Function

    Return the underlying SPICE kernel type.

    source
    SPICEKernels.type — Method
    type(kernel)

    Fallback method to inspect the file extension of the provided kernel, and return the expected kernel type. If the file extension is not recognized, a KeyError is thrown.

    source
    SPICEKernels.C_G_1000012_2012_2017 — Constant

    A SPK kernel of size 143.0 KB, linked from https://naif.jpl.nasa.gov [1]. Calling this variable like a function will return a path to the file, downloading to scratchspace if necessary.

    Extended Help

    This kernel's link was sourced on 2024-10-25.

    References

    [1] https://naif.jpl.nasa.gov/pub/naif/generickernels/spk/comets/CG10000122012_2017.bsp
